3.每位同學皆需選修英文組或日文組16學分，選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。 4.本系最低畢業學分136學分。 5.本系共同必修科目之英語（一）（二）為FL205英文閱讀（一）及FL206英文閱讀（二）英語（三）（四) 為FL235 英文文學導讀（一）及FL236英文文學導讀（二）、英語（六）：英語檢定為FL347外語檢定。 colspan="6">9.「FL347外語檢定」通過門檻分數者，得於每學期期末考前檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免；英文檢定項目或 日文檢定項目未通過者，需持未通過成績單得以選修「EL439英語（六）」或「FL311日語語法分析」課程 抵免。</td><td colspan="3"></td></tr></table>

（105學年度入學新生適用）

105.04.20 一○四學年度第五次教務會議通過

colspan="13"><p>一、「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，共計二學期四學分(為FL140英文（一）、FL141英文(二))。</p><p>二、除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習<strong>主題式英語課程</strong>三學期六學分(為FL244西洋文學概論(3)、FL245英美文學(3))，畢業前需修畢三個不同營隊課程，始取得畢業資格。</p><p>三、英語檢定（2）(為FL347外語檢定)、經典五十（2）、服務學習（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>全民國防教育軍事訓練課程-國際情勢（0）</p></td><td><p>全民國防教育軍事訓練課程-全民國防（0）</p></td><td 自我經營與生涯發展(2)</p></td><td></td><td colspan="11"><p>1.分人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。</p><p>2.學生須於四領域中各選修兩學分課程，共計8學分，其餘二學分由通識講座課程、微課自主學習或通識四大領域課程中選課。應外系學生不得再選人文領域(LE)，須於自然(GN), 生命(LS),社會(GS)三領域中選課</p><p>3. GS418自我經營與生涯發展屬社會科學2學分為應外系學生必修。</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="6"><p>系</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p> (66）</p></td><td .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL140、FL141英文（一）（二）」，「營隊英語及密集先修英語營課程」為「FL244西洋文學概論及FL245英美文學」，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目12學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>5. 以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>6. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>7.「FL347外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公</p><p>    室辦理抵免；96學年度開始一概不接受以課程抵免「FL347外語檢定」。</p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之專業英語課程，請詳「應外系專業英語課程一覽表」。</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。</p><p>11. FL362寫作實務(一)、FL363寫作實務(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>12.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。</p><p>13. 括弧內數字為學分數。</p><p>14. 通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂
```

元智大學 應用外語學系 必修科目表

（106學年度入學新生適用）

Yuan Ze University

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Required Courses

（106學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2017. Sept.\~）

106.04.26 一○五學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on April 26, 2017

106.06.21 一○五學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2016, on June 21, 2017

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>一、「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，共計二學期四學分(為FL140英文（一）、FL141英文(二)。</p><p>(English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters. (FL students are required to take FL140&amp; FL141 instead )</p><p>二、除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習<strong>主題式英語課程</strong>三學期六學分(為FL244西洋文學概論(3)、FL245英美文學(3))，畢業前需修畢三個不同營隊課程，始取得畢業資格。</p><p>English thematic courses are 6- credit of English courses; students are required to obtain 6 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (FL students are required to take FL244&amp; FL245 instead)</p><p>三、大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。(應外系學生未達標準者視同FL141英文(二)不及格)。 The “English Testing” course is provided to students who fail to score 350 in a TOEIC mock held in the end of their first academic year. They will need to take the exam again after the course and pass; otherwise, they will need to take another “English Testing” course next semester. (FL students who didn’t reach the English proficiency requirement is equivalent to fail FL141 English(II) course. )</p><p>三、英語檢定（2）(為FL347外語檢定)、經典五十（2）、服務學習（1）</p><p>English Testing(2) (FL students are required to take FL347 instead)、Fifty Canonized Books（2）、Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 6 semesters (Year 1 to 3), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教</p><p>育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td><p>GS418</p><p>自我經營與生涯發展</p><p>Self-Management and Career Development (2)</p></td><td></td><td colspan="8"><p>1.分人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。</p><p>The General Education program has four Distributive Studies categories :Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science.</p><p>2.學生須於四領域中各選修兩學分課程，共計8學分，其餘2學分學生可自由選擇，由通識講座課程、微課自主學習或通識四大領域課程中選課。應外系學生不得再選人文領域(LE)，須於自然(GN), 生命(LS),社會(GS)三領域中選課。</p><p>Students are required to take a two-credit course from each category to get eight credits before graduation. The rest two credits can be chosen from the General Education Lecture course, Micro- Course &amp; Self-Study or four categories upon their needs. However, there are rules and limitations set by each college for taking a course from the four categories: students of Department of FL cannot choose classes of Humanities (LE), only could choose classes in categories of Natural Science(GN), Life Science(LS) and Social Science(GS). </p><p>3. GS418自我經營與生涯發展屬社會科學2學分為應外系學生必修。</p><p>GS418 Self -Management and Career Development (2 credits) is the required class for FL students.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>系</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Essential </p><p>subjects</p><p>(62）</p></td><td><p>FL142</p><p>跨文化溝通</p><p>Intercultural Communication</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL143</p><p>語言與文化</p><p>Language and Culture</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL250</p><p>進階英文(一)</p><p>Advanced English (I) colspan="8"><p> </p><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p> 2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).英文組：共同必修科目23學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修62學分、分組必修19學分、系選修16學分。</p><p>(2).日文組：共同必修科目23學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修62學分、分組必修19學分、系選修16學分。</p><p>(3).選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。。</p><p>(4).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(5) .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>English group: University Compulsory: 23 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 66 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 22 credits; Department Elective courses: 9 credits</li><li>Japanese group: University Compulsory: 23 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 66 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 12 credits</li><li>If students undertake courses from another group, the credits of the course will be accepted as elective credits. </li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 130 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL140、FL141英文（一）（二）」，「挑戰極限新生英語營」為「FL244西洋文學概論及FL245英美文學」，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。</p><p>  The FL courses which are equivalent to General Education English (I) &amp; (II) are FL140 English (I) and FL141 English (II). The courses equivalent to 「Above &amp; Beyond Freshmen English Program」 are 「FL244 Introduction to Western Literature and FL245 English and American Literature」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL347 Foreign Languages Proficiency」.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目<strong>16</strong>學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. 16 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not include the English/Japanese courses in ILCC and General Studies.</p><p>5. 以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>All courses in Specialized Requirements above are open to all junior and senior students.</p><p>6. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL243 English Outside Reading(IV), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II), FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III) and FL456 Japanese Outside Reading(IV) 」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>7.「FL347外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公</p><p>    室辦理抵免；96學年度開始一概不接受以課程抵免「FL347外語檢定」。</p><p>There is no class for 「FL347 Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL347 Foreign Languages Proficiency」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之專業英語課程，請詳「應外系專業英語課程一覽表」。</p><p>Please refer to 「FL class list of English for Specific purposes」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students.</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。</p><p>「FL381Advanced Japanese (I) and FL382 Advanced Japanese (II) 」 can be waived with 「FL383 Japanese (V) and FL384 Japanese (VI) 」 after students finish two-semester courses. </p><p>11. FL362寫作實務(一)、FL363寫作實務(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>Writing Practicum (I) (1) and FL363 Writing Practicum (II) (1) are capstone courses.</p><p>12.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>13. 括弧內數字為學分數。 Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>14.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂
```

</p><p>(2)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>小</p><p>計</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td><p>7</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td><p>4</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).英文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(2).日文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(3).選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。。</p><p>(4).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(5) .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>English group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>Japanese group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>If students undertake courses from another group, the credits of the course will be accepted as elective credits. </li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 130 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。</p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380 Reading and Discussion and FL465 English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency」. </p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目<strong>17</strong>學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. 17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not include the English/Japanese courses in ILCC and General Studies.</p><p>5. 以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>All courses in Specialized Requirements above are open to all junior and senior students.</p><p>6.「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL243 English Outside Reading(IV), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II), FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III) and FL456 Japanese Outside Reading(IV) 」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>7.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester.</p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之應用英語主題式課程，請詳「應外系應用英語主題式一覽表」。</p><p>Please refer to 「FL class list of English for Specific purposes」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students.</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。</p><p>「FL381Advanced Japanese (I) and FL382 Advanced Japanese (II) 」 can be waived with 「FL383 Japanese (V) and FL384 Japanese (VI) 」 after students finish two-semester courses. </p><p>11. FL268寫作實務(一)、FL363寫作實務(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>Writing Practicum (I) (1) and FL363 Writing Practicum (II) (1) are capstone courses.</p><p>12. FL268寫作實務(一)及FL363寫作實務(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL268 Writing Practicum(I) and FL363Writing Practicum(II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>13. FL269語料庫言談分析、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、數位語音影像編輯、FL378文化創意產業英文為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p> FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis 、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>14.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>15. 括弧內數字為學分數。 Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>16.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂

```markdown
元智大學 應用外語學系 必修科目表

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

110.11.24 一一○學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on November 24, 2021

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>共</p><p>同</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>University Compulsory</p><p>（21）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL380</p><p>閱讀與討論</p><p>Reading and Discussion</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL465英文閱讀與寫作</p><p>English Reading and Writing</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL267</p><p>英文實用</p><p>寫作</p><p>Practical English Writing(2)</p></td><td><p>FL322</p><p>英文商用書信寫作</p><p>English Business Correspond-ence (2)</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。(開課名稱：基礎程式設計)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming is a four-credit course. For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註7）</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3) </li></ol><p>Students who do not reach the 350 points threshold of the English posttest in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><ol><li>English Test for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 7)</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).  </p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）     </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教</p><p>育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><ol><li>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</li><li>應外系學生社會科學領域必修GS418自我經營與生涯發展。FL students take GS418 Self -Management and Career Development (2 credits) as the required course in Social Science category.</li><li>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士學位學程、資訊學院英語學士學位學程、人文社會學院英語學士學位學程、電機通訊學院英語學士學位學程學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation. </li></ol></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).英文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(2).日文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(3).選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。。</p><p>(4).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(5) .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>English group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>Japanese group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>If students undertake courses from another group, the credits of the course will be accepted as elective credits. </li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 130 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格] </p><p>    The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目<strong>17</strong>學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. 17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not include the English/Japanese courses in ILCC and General Studies.</p><p>5.以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>All courses in Specialized Requirements above are open to all junior and senior students.</p><p>6.「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL243 English Outside Reading(IV), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II), FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III) and FL456 Japanese Outside Reading(IV) 」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>7.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester.<s> </s></p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。. </p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same</p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之應用英語主題式課程，請詳「應外系應用英語主題式一覽表」。</p><p>Please refer to 「FL class list of English for Specific purposes」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students.</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。「FL381Advanced Japanese (I) and FL382 Advanced Japanese (II) 」 can be waived with 「FL383 Japanese (V) and FL384 Japanese (VI) 」 after students finish two-semester courses. </p><p>11. FL268寫作實務(一)、FL363寫作實務(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>Writing Practicum (I) (1) and FL363 Writing Practicum (II) (1) are capstone courses.</p><p>12. FL268寫作實務(一)及FL363寫作實務(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL268 Writing Practicum(I) and FL363Writing Practicum(II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>13. FL269語料庫言談分析、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、數位語音影像編輯、FL378文化創意產業英文為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p> FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis 、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>14.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 </p><p>Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>15. 括弧內數字為學分數。 </p><p>Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>16.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</p><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂
```

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>共</p><p>同</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>University Compulsory</p><p>（21）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL380</p><p>閱讀與討論</p><p>Reading and Discussion</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL465英文閱讀與寫作</p><p>English Reading and Writing (2)</p></td><td><p>FL267</p><p>英文實用寫作Practical English Writing(2)</p></td><td><p>FL322</p><p>英文商用書信寫作</p><p>English Business Correspond-ence (2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。(開課名稱：基礎程式設計)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming is a four-credit course. For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註7）</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3) </li></ol><p>Students who do not reach the 350 points threshold of the English posttest in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><ol><li>English Test for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 7)</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).  </p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教</p><p>育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</li><li>應外系學生社會科學領域必修GS418自我經營與生涯發展。FL students take GS418 Self -Management and Career Development (2 credits) as the required course in Social Science category.</li><li>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士學位學程、資訊學院英語學士學位學程、人文社會學院英語學士學位學程、電機通訊學院英語學士學位學程學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation..</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="7"><p>系</p><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>Essential </p><p>subjects</p><p>(63）</p></td><td><p>FL151</p><p>跨文化溝通</p><p>Intercultural Communication</p><p> colspan="8"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).英文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(2).日文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(3).選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。。</p><p>(4).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(5) .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>English group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>Japanese group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>If students undertake courses from another group, the credits of the course will be accepted as elective credits. </li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 130 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>  The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目<strong>17</strong>學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. 17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not include the English/Japanese courses in ILCC and General Studies.</p><p>5. 以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>All courses in Specialized Requirements above are open to all junior and senior students.</p><p>6. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL243 English Outside Reading(IV), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II), FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III) and FL456 Japanese Outside Reading(IV) 」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>7.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. </p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之應用英語主題式課程，請詳「應外系應用英語主題式一覽表」，超修之學分可認列系選修學分。</p><p>Please refer to「FL class list of English for Specific purposes 」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students. Extra credits taken beyond the required eight credits will be recognized as Department elective credits.</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。</p><p>「FL381Advanced Japanese (I) and FL382 Advanced Japanese (II) 」 can be waived with 「FL383 Japanese (V) and FL384 Japanese (VI) 」 after students finish two-semester courses. </p><p>11. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>12. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>13. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究、為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>14.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>15. 括弧內數字為學分數。 Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>16.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>17.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂

Please refer to「FL class list of English for Specific purposes 」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students. <table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="6"><p>共同必修科目</p><p>University Compulsory</p><p>（21）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL380</p><p>閱讀與討論</p><p>Reading and Discussion</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL465</p><p>英文閱讀與寫作</p><p>English Reading and Writing (2)</p></td><td><p>FL267</p><p>英文實用</p><p>寫作 Practical English Writing(2)</p></td><td><p>FL322</p><p>英文商用書信寫作</p><p>English Business Correspond-ence (2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。(開課名稱：基礎程式設計)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming is a four-credit course. For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註7）</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3) </li></ol><p>Students who do not reach the 350 points threshold of the English posttest in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><ol><li>English Test for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 7)</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).  </p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses, students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><ol><li>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</li><li>應外系學生社會科學領域必修GS418自我經營與生涯發展。FL students take GS418 Self -Management and Career Development (2 credits) as the required course in Social Science category.</li><li>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士學位學程、資訊學院英語學士學位學程、人文社會學院英語學士學位學程、電機通訊學院英語學士學位學程學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="7"><p>系必修科目</p><p>Essential colspan="8"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).英文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(2).日文組：共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修63學分、分組必修19學分、系選修17學分。</p><p>(3).選修他組課程者，該科將以選修課程的方式承認。。</p><p>(4).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(5) .總計不得低於130學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>English group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>Japanese group: University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 63 credits; Group Compulsory courses: 19 credits; Department Elective courses: 17 credits</li><li>If students undertake courses from another group, the credits of the course will be accepted as elective credits. </li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 130 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>  The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認；選修科目<strong>17</strong>學分可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. 17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not include the English/Japanese courses in ILCC and General Studies.</p><p>5. 以上分組必修課程三、四年級皆可選修。</p><p>All courses in Specialized Requirements above are open to all junior and senior students.</p><p>6. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL243英文課外閱讀(四)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」<s>、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL456日文課外閱讀(四)」</s>為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL243 English Outside Reading(IV), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II)<s>, FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III) and FL456 Japanese Outside Reading(IV) </s>」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>7.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. </p><p>8.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>9. 大三、大四必修之應用英語主題式課程，請詳「應外系應用英語主題式一覽表」，超修之學分可認列系選修學分。</p><p>Please refer to「FL class list of English for Specific purposes 」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students. Extra credits taken beyond the required eight credits will be recognized as Department elective credits.</p><p>10.「進階日語(一)(二)」可以「日語(五)(六)」抵免，需修完兩學期的課才可申請抵免。</p><p>「FL381Advanced Japanese (I) and FL382 Advanced Japanese (II) 」 can be waived with 「FL383 Japanese (V) and FL384 Japanese (VI) 」 after students finish two-semester courses. </p><p>11. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>12. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>13. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究、為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>14.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>15. 括弧內數字為學分數。 Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>16.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>17.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.04.19修訂

Credits are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>2. All courses above are open to all junior and senior students except for those who cannot fulfill the prerequisites.</p><p>3 .Elective courses will only be opened once every two years.</p><p>4. Master classes are partly open to undergraduate students, credits are the same as the selective classes.</p><p>5. Please refer to「FL class list of English for Specific purposes 」 for courses in Specialized Requirements for junior and senior students. Extra credits taken beyond the required eight credits will be recognized as Department elective credits.</p></td></tr></table>

(See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1).共同必修科目21學分、通識教育科目10學分、系必修67學分、模組課程13學分、自由選修17學分(可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2).選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3).有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4).總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p>Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li> University Compulsory: 21 credits; General Education courses: 10credits; Department Compulsory courses: 67 credits; Modular courses: 13 credits; Elective courses: 17 credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not including  English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>  The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」<s>、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」</s>為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II), FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I)<s>,</s> <s>FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II) and FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III)</s>」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>6.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>7.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>8. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) (1) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) (1) are capstone courses.</p><p>9.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究、為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>11.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。 Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>12. 括弧內數字為學分數。 Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>13.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>14.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／110.10.19修訂

元智大學 應用外語學系 必修科目表

（112學年度入學新生適用）

Yuan Ze University

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Required Courses

（Academic Year 2023. Sept.\~）

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on November 22, 2023

<table><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td><td><p>上</p><p>Fall</p></td><td><p>下</p><p>Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目</p><p>Common Compulsory（17）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL380</p><p>閱讀與討論</p><p>Reading and Discussion</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL465英文閱讀與寫作</p><p>English Reading and Writing (2)</p></td><td><p>FL267</p><p>英文實用寫作Practical English Writing(2)</p></td><td><p>FL322</p><p>英文商用書信寫作</p><p>English Business Correspond-ence (2)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。（備註3）</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註6）</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 6)</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics (2)、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory（4）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。</p><p>The Fundamental Computer Programming has 4 credits in total, which is subject to the rules of each college.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" rowspan="8"><p>系必修科目</p><p>Essential </p><p>subjects</p><p>（67）</p></td><td><p>FL119</p><p>資訊概論 Introduction to Information Technology (2)</p></td><td><p>FL153</p><p>科技輔助語言學習 Technology-Enhanced Language Learning(2)</p></td><td colspan="6"><p>專業職場課程至少13學分</p><p>Language for Specific Purposes courses at least 13 credits.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL313</p><p>英語溝通技巧</p><p>English Communicatio-n Technique </p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>FL442</p><p>英語簡報技巧 English Presentation Skills (0)</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修67學分、模組課程13學分、自由選修17學分(可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (67) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (17) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」<s>、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」</s>為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II)<s>, FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II) and FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III)</s>」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>6.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>7.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>8. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>9.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究、為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>11.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>12. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>13.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>14.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>15.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／110.10.19修訂
```

元智大學 應用外語學系 選修科目表

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics at Yuan Ze University List of Elective Courses

（112學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2023. Sept.\~）

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

113.11.20 一一三學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on November 20, 2024

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on December 24, 2025

(II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 6)</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p></td><td><p>12</p></td><td><p>12</p></td><td><p>12</p></td><td><p>11</p></td><td><p><strong>0+2</strong></p></td><td><p><strong>2+2</strong></p></td><td><p><strong>1+2</strong></p></td><td><p><strong>0+2</strong></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修67學分、模組課程13學分、自由選修17學分(可於外系修習、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (67) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (17) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程5學分為EL163大一先修英語(1)、FL267英文實用寫作(2)及 FL322英文商用書信寫作(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL400外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL267 Practical English Writing and FL322 English Business Correspondence」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL400 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5. 「FL134英文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL135英文課外閱讀(二)」<s>、「FL242英文課外閱讀(三)」、「FL358日文課外閱讀(一)」、「FL359日文課外閱讀(二) 」、「FL455日文課外閱讀(三)」</s>為共同必修，若有未修完之課程則不得畢業。</p><p>「FL134 English Outside Reading(I), FL135 English Outside Reading(II)<s>, FL242 English Outside Reading(III), FL358 Japanese Outside Reading(I), FL359 Japanese Outside Reading(II) and FL455 Japanese Outside Reading(III)</s>」 are Department Compulsory courses which are required for graduation.</p><p>6.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>7.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>8. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>9.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>10. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究、為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>11.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>12. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>13.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>14.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>15.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／110.10.19修訂

元智大學 應用外語學系 必修科目表

（113學年度入學新生適用）

Yuan Ze University

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Required Courses

（Academic Year 2024. Sept.\~）

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 9th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on June 05, 2024

colspan="13"><ol><li>外語課程應修習 10 學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。（備註3）</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註5）</li><li>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程 10 學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 5)</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> <strong>英語檢定English Testing （2）</strong>、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="13"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="13"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td
