colspan="2"><p><strong>0+2</strong></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="15"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修48學分、模組課程13學分、選修36學分(外系選修至多承認17學分、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (48) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (36) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程4學分為<s> </s>FL373演說與辯論(2)及FL439商務溝通(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL 373 Speech and Debate and FL439 Business Communication」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL347 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>6.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>7. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>8.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究，為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>10.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>11. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>12.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>13.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>14.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>15.修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／110.10.19修訂
```

元智大學 應用外語學系 選修科目表

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics at Yuan Ze University List of Elective Courses

（113學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2024. Sept.\~）

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on November 20, 2024

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 4th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on December 24, 2025

(See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education. complete 1 of the 2 elective course modules (at least 13 credits).</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>9</p></td><td colspan="2"><p><strong>0+2</strong></p></td><td colspan="2"><p><strong>2+2</strong></p></td><td colspan="2"><p><strong>1+2</strong></p></td><td colspan="2"><p><strong>0+2</strong></p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="15"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修48學分、模組課程13學分、選修36學分(外系選修至多承認17學分、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (48) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (36) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程4學分為<s> </s>FL373演說與辯論(2)及FL439商務溝通(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL 373 Speech and Debate and FL439 Business Communication」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL347 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>6.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>7. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>8.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究，為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>10.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>11. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>12.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>13.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>14.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>15.修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／110.10.19修訂

元智大學 應用外語學系 必修科目表

（114學年度入學新生適用）

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics, Yuan Ze University

List of Required Courses

（Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2025）

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

學分。</li><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。（備註3）</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢二個不同主題式英語課程，共計 4 學分。（備註3）</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC 模擬測驗」成績未達 350 分者，應修習「應試加強班」（EL260）。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末 TOEIC 模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註5）</li><li>外國學生可修華語課程10學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 5)</li><li>Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese （I） and （II） before taking Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV）. Students must pass Mandarin Chinese （III） and （IV） before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> 英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p><a></a>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td><p>數位人文應用（一）</p><p>Digital Applications in Humanities I</p><p>(2)</p></td><td><p>數位人文應用（二）</p><p>Digital Applications colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td><p>9</p></td><td><p>0+2</p></td><td><p>2+2</p></td><td><p>1+2</p></td><td><p>0+2</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修48學分、模組課程13學分、自由選修36學分(外系選修至多承認17學分，含專業自主學習至多3學分、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (48) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (36) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, including up to 3 credits from disciplinary self-directed learning, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程4學分為<s> </s>FL373演說與辯論(2)及FL439商務溝通(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL 373 Speech and Debate and FL439 Business Communication」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL347 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>6.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>7. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>8.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究，為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>10.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>11. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>12.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>13.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>14.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>15.修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂
```

模擬測驗成績未達 350 分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達 350 分（含）始得修習其他主題式英語課程。（備註3）</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」（EL160）計一學期2學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。（備註5）</li><li>外國學生可修華語課程10學分，其華語課程 10 學分應含「華語檢定」2 學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」及「元智大學外籍生華語學分抵免規定」。</li><li>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語檢定」（EL375）。</li><li>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</li><li>English （I） &amp; （II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters. (See remark 3)</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. (See remark 3)</li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. (See remark 3)</li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education. (See remark 5)</li><li>Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. colspan="2"><p>學期學分小計</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td><p>8</p></td><td><p>10</p></td><td><p>9</p></td><td><p>0+2</p></td><td><p>2+2</p></td><td><p>1+2</p></td><td><p>0+2</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>1.有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><p>2.欲取得應用外語學系主修之學生必須完成以下課程：</p><p>(1)共同必修科目17學分、通識教育科目10學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、系必修48學分、模組課程13學分、自由選修36學分(外系選修至多承認17學分，含專業自主學習至多3學分、但不含語言中心英、日語課程及通識課程)。</p><p>(2)選修模組二選一，每種至少13學分。</p><p>(3)有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</p><p>(4)總計不得低於128學分始得畢業。</p><p> Student of Dept. of FL are required to undertake courses below:</p><ol><li>University Compulsory (17) credits, General Education courses (10) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (48) credits, Modular courses (13) credits, Elective courses (36) credits. (17 credits of selective courses can be undertaken in other departments, including up to 3 credits from disciplinary self-directed learning, however, not including English/Japanese courses in ILCC and courses in General Studies.)</li><li>Among 2 Elective course modules, students have to complete 1 modules (at least 13 credits for each module).</li><li>About subjects of University Compulsory and General Education, please refer to 「Yuan Ze University List of Required Courses」for details.</li><li>A minimum of 128 credit hours are required for graduation.</li></ol><p>3. 本系共同必修科目之「英語（一）（二）」為「FL380閱讀與討論、FL465英文閱讀與寫作」，主題式英語課程4學分為<s> </s>FL373演說與辯論(2)及FL439商務溝通(2)，「英語檢定」為「FL347外語檢定」。[應外系學生TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者視同FL465英文閱讀與寫作不合格]      </p><p>The FL courses which are equivalent to「 General Education English (I) &amp; (II) 」 are 「FL380Reading and Discussion and FL465English Reading and Writing」. The courses equivalent to 「English thematic course」 are 「FL 373 Speech and Debate and FL439 Business Communication」, and 「English Proficiency」 are 「FL347 Foreign Language Proficiency 」. The FL students will fail the course FL465 if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course.</p><p>4. 本系必修科目必須在系上修習方予承認，如有特殊原因需至外系修習者，需於選課時經系主任核准，其學分始得承認。</p><p>Department Compulsory and Elective courses must be undertaken within the department, if an individual needs to undertake any of them in other departments, the credits can be admitted only when it’s been approved by the Department Chair. </p><p>5.「外語檢定」不開設課程、直接抵免。同學得於通過畢業門檻該學期期末考前ㄧ週檢附成績單至系辦公室辦理抵免。</p><p>There is no class for 「Foreign Languages Proficiency」. Students can apply for credits waive with the report card handed in to the office one week before the finals of each semester. Courses will not be waived for credits of 「FL473 English Test &amp; FL474 Japanese Language Proficiency Test」 after 2007 academic year any more.</p><p>6.「日語演說(一)/(二)」與「日語習作(一) /(二)」為套裝課程，授課教師同一人。</p><p>「Japanese Speech (I) &amp; (II) and Japanese Writing Practice (I) &amp; (II) 」are modular courses, and the instructor will be the same. </p><p>7. FL475畢業專題(一)、FL476畢業專題(二)為終端學習課程。</p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) are capstone courses.</p><p>8.FL475畢業專題(一)及FL476畢業專題(二)為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </p><p>FL475 Graduation Project (I) and FL476 Graduation Project (II) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><p>9. FL219數位翻譯應用、FL248英文筆譯實務、FL269語料庫言談分析、FL378文化創意產業英文、FL388日語簡報技巧、FL407電腦輔助教學、FL408多媒體教材製作、FL458日本研究，為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</p><p>FL219 Digital Application of Translation、FL248 English Translation in Practice、FL269 Corpus Based Discourse Analysis、FL378 English for Cultural and Creative Industries、FL388 Japanese Presentation Skills、FL407 Computer Assistant Instruction、FL408 Multimedia Teaching material Production、FL458 Japanese Studies are courses of 'Digital Application Courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><p>10.「學期學分小計」指系必修科目學分數之合計。Semester Subtotal is the requirement of total credit hours.</p><p>11. 括弧內數字為學分數。Credit hours are indicated in parentheses.</p><p>12.通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><p>13.為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</p><p>To improve students＇ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor) , which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><p>14.自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</p><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><p>15.修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</p><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂
```

#### OCR 93: files/COURSES/601FL/109FL-extend.docx

- 關聯類型: 超連結（檔案）
- 本機檔案: admin/aa/files/COURSES/601FL/109FL-extend.docx

```markdown
**元智大學應用外語系輔系科目表**

Yuan Ze University

Department of Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Minor Courses

（109學年度申請通過學生適用）

（For Students Apply to Academic Year 2020）

110.05.05 一○九學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2020, on May 05, 2021

**A. 申請資格及規定Qualifications and Regulations for Applicants**

1. 外系輔系分為「英文組」及「日文組」。

Minor in Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics are divided into English group and Japanese group.

2. 欲申請的同學需於每學期初依照教務處規定時程完成申請手續。

Applicants must complete the application procedures by the scheduled time given by the Office of Academic Affairs at the beginning of the semester.

3. 申請資格： (1) 上學期成績總平均須達75分以上。

(2) 需檢附歷年成績單(有排名)，及相關有利之英、日文檢定證明。

Qualifications for the Applicant：

(1) Must be sophomore or above.

(2) GPA of previous semester must be 75 or higher.

(3) Hand in the transcript (with ranking) and relevant English and Japanese Language Proficiency Certificate.

4. 招收名額：每學期、每組各 2 名，若申請人數超過招收名額則另行開會決議。Enrollment Figure: 2 applicants will be accepted for each group every semester. If the applicants exceed the quota, the issue will be discussed and decided through a meeting of the department.
5. 本系設有擋修規定，標有（一）（二）之上下連貫課程需皆修畢才得承認4學分，相關規定請考本系擋修科目表。

Courses with (I) (II) are prerequisites and students have to pass both courses to receive 4 credits. Refer to the list of courses of the department for more details.

6. 於本學程內修讀之科目不得重疊列入學生原系之畢業學分範圍內。

Credits taken in this program are not included in the graduation requirement of the student’s major.

7. 選修本系為輔系之學生必須滿 36 (含)學分以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Minor in this department will only be given when student received 36 credits.

8. 以上事項若有未盡事宜，則由應用外語系系務會議開會後決定。

Any unresolved issues will be decided in the Foreign Language and Applied Linguistic Departmental Affair Council Meeting.

**B. 應用外語輔系科目一覽表**

**List of courses for Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics Minor:**

110.11.24 一一○學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on November 24, 2021

**A. 申請資格及規定Qualifications and Regulations for Applicants**

1. 輔系分為「英文組」及「日文組」。

Minor in Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics are divided into English group and Japanese group.

2. 欲申請的同學需於每學期初依照教務處規定時程完成申請手續。

**元智大學應用外語系輔系科目表**

Yuan Ze University

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Minor Courses

（111學年度申請通過學生適用）

（For Students Apply to Academic Year 2022）

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 20, 2022

**A. 申請資格及規定Qualifications and Regulations for Applicants**

1. 輔系分為「英文組」及「日文組」。

Minor in Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics are divided into English group and Japanese group.

2. 欲申請的同學需於每學期初依照教務處規定時程完成申請手續。

Applicants must complete the application procedures by the scheduled time given by the Office of Academic Affairs at the beginning of the semester.

3. 本系設有擋修規定，標有（一）（二）之上下連貫課程需皆修畢才得承認4學分，相關規定請考本系擋修科目表。

Courses with (I) (II) are prerequisites and students have to pass both courses to receive 4 credits. Refer to the list of courses of the department for more details.

4. 於本學程內修讀之科目不得重疊列入學生原系之畢業學分範圍內。

Credits taken in this program are not included in the graduation requirement of the student’s major.

5. 選修本系為輔系之學生必須滿30 (含)學分以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Minor in this department will only be given when student received ~~36~~ credits.

6. 以上事項若有未盡事宜，則由應用外語系系務會議開會後決定。

Any unresolved issues will be decided in the Foreign Language and Applied Linguistic Departmental Affair Council Meeting.

```markdown
**元智大學應用外語系輔系科目表**

Yuan Ze University

Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics

List of Minor Courses

（113學年度申請通過學生適用）

（For Students Apply to Academic Year 2024）

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

**A. 申請資格及規定Qualifications and Regulations for Applicants**

1. 輔系分為「英文組」及「日文組」。

Minor in Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics are divided into English group and Japanese group.

2. 欲申請的同學需於每學期初依照教務處規定時程完成申請手續。

Applicants must complete the application procedures by the scheduled time given by the Office of Academic Affairs at the beginning of the semester.

3. 本系設有擋修規定，標有（一）（二）之上下連貫課程需皆修畢才得承認4學分，相關規定請考本系擋修科目表。

Courses with (I) (II) are prerequisites and students have to pass both courses to receive 4 credits. Refer to the list of courses of the department for more details.

4. 於本學程內修讀之科目不得重疊列入學生原系之畢業學分範圍內。

Credits taken in this program are not included in the graduation requirement of the student’s major.

5. 選修本系為輔系之學生必須滿20 (含)學分以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

Minor in this department will only be given when student received 20 credits.

6. 以上事項若有未盡事宜，則由應用外語系系務會議開會後決定。

Any unresolved issues will be decided in the Foreign Language and Applied Linguistic Departmental Affair Council Meeting.

**B. 應用外語輔系科目一覽表**

**List of courses for Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics Minor:**

**必修科目表**

**Master Program of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics Department at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

Please refer to the 「Language Requirement for Master of the Department of Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics」for more details.</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Graduate students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多3學分可於外系或外校修課，須經過系課程委員會議通過才可選課，若指導教授因</li></ol><p>碩士論文之需求要求學生於外系或外校選課則可例外；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</p><p>After getting approval from the Curriculum Committee of the department, students can get three elective credits at most from other departments or universities; students who are asked by their advisors to take courses from other departments or universities for master thesis are exempted; courses available in the department are not allowed to take in other departments or universities.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」</li></ol><p>For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

Please refer to the 「Language Requirement for Master of the Department of Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics」for more details.</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Graduate students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多3學分可於外系或外校修課，須經過系課程委員會議通過才可選課，若指導教授因</li></ol><p>碩士論文之需求要求學生於外系或外校選課則可例外；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</p><p>After getting approval from the Curriculum Committee of the department, students can get three elective credits at most from other departments or universities; students who are asked by their advisors to take courses from other departments or universities for master thesis are exempted; courses available in the department are not allowed to take in other departments or universities.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」</li></ol><p>For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

Practice</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL613</p></td><td><p>教材與課程設計</p></td><td><p>Language Teaching Materials and Course Design</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL615</p></td><td><p>專業演說與寫作</p></td><td><p>Professional Presentation and Writing</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註 </p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>凡修習他所課程，選課前須先徵詢授課老師和導師同意，並提請所務會議核備後，始承認該學分。</li></ol><p>Credits from other departments will be accepted only after getting approval from students’ mentors, advisors and department committee. </p><ol><li>選修科目視當年度需求開設。</li></ol><p>Elective courses will be opened based on students’ needs in that year.  </p><ol><li>以上選修科目，碩一、碩二學生皆可選修。</li></ol><p>Above elective courses are available for both of the first and the second year students in Master program.  </p></td></tr></table>

**必修科目表**

**Master Program of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics Department at Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（112學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2023. Sept.\~）**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on April 19, 2023

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議通過

Amended by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on May 31, 2023

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必</p><p>修</p><p>科</p><p>目</p><p>（9）</p><p>Compulsory courses</p><p>（9）</p></td><td><p>FL563</p><p>英文寫作</p><p>English Writing </p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>研究方法</p><p> Research Methodologies</p><p> (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td><p>FL607</p><p>專題研究</p><p>Special Topics </p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>6</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li><a></a>最低畢業學分 27 學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 27 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目9學分、選修科目18學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 9 credits; elective courses: 18 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>英語能力要求：本所學生必須於畢業前自行參加英語言能力測驗，檢定標準請參考「元智大學應用外語學系檢定規定」之規定。</li></ol><p>English proficiency: Students in this graduate school need to attend and pass the English proficiency test before graduation. Please refer to the 「Language Requirement of the Department of Foreign Language and Applied Linguistics」for more details.</p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Graduate students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多3學分可於外系或外校修課，須經過系課程委員會議通過才可選課，若指導教授因碩士論文之需求要求學生於外系或外校選課則可例外；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</li></ol><p>After getting approval from the Curriculum Committee of the department, students can get three elective credits at most from other departments or universities; students who are asked by their advisors to take courses from other departments or universities for master thesis are exempted; courses available in the department are not allowed to take in other departments or universities.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」</li></ol><p>For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p><ol><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ol><p>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

**必修科目表**

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

**Department of Foreign Languages and Applied Linguistics, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses for the Master Program**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2025）**

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>  學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Course</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修科目</p><p>（6）</p><p>Required course</p><p>（6）</p></td><td><p>FL595</p><p>AI輔助學術論文寫作</p><p> AI-Assisted Academic Writing</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>研究方法</p><p> Research Methodologies</p><p> (3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li><a></a>最低畢業學分 24 學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 24 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目6學分、選修科目18學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 9 credits; elective courses: 15 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Graduate students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多9學分可於外系或外校修課，須經指導教授同意；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</li></ol><p>Students can get 9 elective credits at most from other departments or universities with approval by their advisor. Students cannot take courses available in the department.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」</li></ol><p>For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p><ol><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ol><p>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

```markdown
**元智大學　應用外語學系碩士班**

**必修科目表**

**（115學年度入學新生適用）**

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議通過

Passed by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on April 29, 2026

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>  學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Course</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必修科目</p><p>（6）</p><p>Required course</p><p>（6）</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>FL595</p><p>AI輔助學術論文寫作</p><p> AI-Assisted Academic Writing</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL544</p><p>研究方法：質性分析</p><p> Qualitive Research Method</p><p> (3)</p></td><td rowspan="2"></td><td rowspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td><p>FL550</p><p>研究方法：量化分析</p><p> Quantitative Research Method</p><p> (3)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備</p><p>註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li><a></a>最低畢業學分 24 學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 24 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目6學分( FL595 AI輔助學術論文寫作、FL544研究方法：質性分析或FL550研究方法：量化分析)、選修科目18學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 6 credits(FL595 AI-Assisted Academic Writing、FL544 Qualitive Research Method or FL550 Quantitative Research Method ); elective courses: 18 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>若FL544研究方法：質性分析或FL550研究方法：量化分析均修者，其中3學分為必修學分，另3學分得認列為選修學分。</li></ol><p>If the Qualitive Research Method and Quantitative Research Method were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Graduate students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多9學分可於外系或外校修課，須經指導教授同意；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</li></ol><p>Students can get 9 elective credits at most from other departments or universities with approval by their advisor. Students cannot take courses available in the department.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」</li></ol><p>For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p><ol><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ol><p>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

elective courses: 21 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Master students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多3學分可於外系或外校修課，須經過系課程委員會議通過才可選課，若指導教授</li></ol><p>因碩士論文之需求要求學生於外系或外校選課則可例外；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或</p><p>外校修課。</p><p>After getting approval from the Curriculum Committee of the department, students can get three elective credits at most from other departments or universities; students who are asked by their advisors to take courses from other departments or universities for master thesis are exempted; courses available in the department are not allowed to take in other departments or universities.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」For those Graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

**必修科目表**

**Master Program of Languages and Applied Linguistics Department at Yuan Ze University (Part-time)**

**List of Required Courses**

**（111學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2022. Sept.\~）**

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 20, 2022

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必修科目</p><p>（6）</p><p>Compulsory courses</p><p>（6）</p></td><td><p>FL570</p><p>論文寫作指導（一）</p><p>Guided Practice in Research Writing I</p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL571</p><p>論文寫作指導（二）</p><p>Guided Practice in Research Writing II</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分<strong> 27</strong>學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 27 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目<strong>6</strong>學分、選修科目<strong>21</strong>學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 6 credits; elective courses: 21 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Master students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多3學分可於外系或外校修課，須經過系課程委員會議通過才可選課，若指導教授</li></ol><p>因碩士論文之需求要求學生於外系或外校選課則可例外；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或</p><p>外校修課。</p><p>After getting approval from the Curriculum Committee of the department, students can get three elective credits at most from other departments or universities; students who are asked by their advisors to take courses from other departments or universities for master thesis are exempted; courses available in the department are not allowed to take in other departments or universities.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」For those Graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

available for both of the first and the second year students in Master program.  </p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂
```

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

Passed by the 8th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on May 01, 2024

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修科目</p><p>（6）</p><p>Compulsory courses</p><p>（6）</p></td><td><p>FL511</p><p>研究方法</p><p>Research Methodologies </p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL574</p><p>日語文獻解讀</p><p>Literature Review in Japanese</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分<strong> 24</strong>學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 24 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目<strong>6</strong>學分、選修科目<strong>18</strong>學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 6 credits; elective courses: 18 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Master students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多6學分可於外系或外校修課，須經指導教授同意；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</li></ol><p>Students can get 6 elective credits at most from other departments or universities with approval by their advisor. Students cannot take courses available in the department.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」For those Graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ol><p>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學　應用外語學系碩士(在職進修專班)**

**必修科目表**

**Master Program of Languages and Applied Linguistics Department at Yuan Ze University (Part-time)**

**List of Required Courses**

**（114學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2025. Sept.\~）**

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通過

Passed by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2024, on April 23, 2025

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期<br/>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Course</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td><td><p>上 Fall</p></td><td><p>下 Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>必修科目</p><p>（6）</p><p>Required course</p><p>（6）</p></td><td><p>FL511</p><p>研究方法</p><p>Research Methodologies </p><p>(3)</p></td><td><p>FL574</p><p>日語文獻解讀</p><p>Literature Review in Japanese</p><p>(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計</p><p>Credits each semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分<strong> 24</strong>學分 （＋碩士論文）。</li></ol><p>Students must take a minimum of 24 credits and complete one master thesis for graduation.</p><ol><li>必修科目<strong>6</strong>學分、選修科目<strong>18</strong>學分、碩士論文0學分。</li></ol><p>Compulsory courses: 6 credits; elective courses: 18 credits; master thesis: 0 credit</p><ol><li>非相關科系畢業之研究生，由「碩士班委員會」個案核定應補修課程。</li></ol><p>Students who are not from the related departments need to make up for the courses decided by the Masters Committee. </p><ol><li>研究生於報到後由「碩士班委員會」安排「課程指導教授」指導第一年修課事宜。</li></ol><p>Master students will be assigned to a mentor individually by the Masters Committee for guiding the courses in the first year after their enrollment. </p><ol><li>選修科目最多6學分可於外系或外校修課，須經指導教授同意；本系有開設課程一律不允許於外系或外校修課。</li></ol><p>Students can get 6 elective credits at most from other departments or universities with approval by their advisor. Students cannot take courses available in the department.</p><ol><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。」For those Graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</li><li>欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</li></ol><p>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂
